M r θ : ℝ
h_ext : Exterior M r θ
h_θ : sin θ ≠ 0
a b : Idx
compat_r_a_e :
  ∀ (e : Idx),
    dCoord Idx.r (fun r θ => g M a e r θ) r θ =
      (sumIdx fun k => Γtot M r θ k Idx.r a * g M k e r θ) + sumIdx fun k => Γtot M r θ k Idx.r e * g M a k r θ
compat_θ_a_e :
  ∀ (e : Idx),
    dCoord Idx.θ (fun r θ => g M a e r θ) r θ =
      (sumIdx fun k => Γtot M r θ k Idx.θ a * g M k e r θ) + sumIdx fun k => Γtot M r θ k Idx.θ e * g M a k r θ
H₁ :
  (sumIdx fun k => Γtot M r θ k Idx.θ b * sumIdx fun lam => Γtot M r θ lam Idx.r k * g M a lam r θ) =
    sumIdx fun k => g M a k r θ * sumIdx fun lam => Γtot M r θ k Idx.r lam * Γtot M r θ lam Idx.θ b
H₂ :
  (sumIdx fun k => Γtot M r θ k Idx.r b * sumIdx fun lam => Γtot M r θ lam Idx.θ k * g M a lam r θ) =
    sumIdx fun k => g M a k r θ * sumIdx fun lam => Γtot M r θ k Idx.θ lam * Γtot M r θ lam Idx.r b
f1 : Idx → ℝ := fun k => dCoord Idx.r (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ k Idx.θ b) r θ * g M a k r θ
f2 : Idx → ℝ := fun k => dCoord Idx.θ (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ k Idx.r b) r θ * g M a k r θ
f3 : Idx → ℝ := fun k => Γtot M r θ k Idx.θ b * sumIdx fun k₁ => Γtot M r θ k₁ Idx.r a * g M k₁ k r θ
f4 : Idx → ℝ := fun k => Γtot M r θ k Idx.θ b * sumIdx fun k₁ => Γtot M r θ k₁ Idx.r k * g M a k₁ r θ
f5 : Idx → ℝ := fun k => Γtot M r θ k Idx.r b * sumIdx fun k₁ => Γtot M r θ k₁ Idx.θ a * g M k₁ k r θ
f6 : Idx → ℝ := fun k => Γtot M r θ k Idx.r b * sumIdx fun k₁ => Γtot M r θ k₁ Idx.θ k * g M a k₁ r θ
goal_shape :
  (fun k =>
      dCoord Idx.r (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ k Idx.θ b) r θ * g M a k r θ +
            -(dCoord Idx.θ (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ k Idx.r b) r θ * g M a k r θ) +
          ((Γtot M r θ k Idx.θ b * sumIdx fun k_1 => Γtot M r θ k_1 Idx.r a * g M k_1 k r θ) +
            Γtot M r θ k Idx.θ b * sumIdx fun k_1 => Γtot M r θ k_1 Idx.r k * g M a k_1 r θ) +
        -((Γtot M r θ k Idx.r b * sumIdx fun k_1 => Γtot M r θ k_1 Idx.θ a * g M k_1 k r θ) +
            Γtot M r θ k Idx.r b * sumIdx fun k_1 => Γtot M r θ k_1 Idx.θ k * g M a k_1 r θ)) =
    fun k => f1 k - f2 k + (f3 k + f4 k) - (f5 k + f6 k)
split6 :
  (sumIdx fun k => f1 k - f2 k + (f3 k + f4 k) - (f5 k + f6 k)) =
    sumIdx f1 - sumIdx f2 + (sumIdx f3 + sumIdx f4) - (sumIdx f5 + sumIdx f6)
shape_identify_r_left :
  (sumIdx fun k => Γtot M r θ k Idx.θ b * sumIdx fun σ => Γtot M r θ σ Idx.r a * g M σ k r θ) =
    sumIdx fun ρ => (sumIdx fun σ => Γtot M r θ σ Idx.r a * g M σ ρ r θ) * Γtot M r θ ρ Idx.θ b
shape_identify_θ_left :
  (sumIdx fun k => Γtot M r θ k Idx.r b * sumIdx fun σ => Γtot M r θ σ Idx.θ a * g M σ k r θ) =
    sumIdx fun ρ => (sumIdx fun σ => Γtot M r θ σ Idx.θ a * g M σ ρ r θ) * Γtot M r θ ρ Idx.r b
branch_r_merge :
  sumIdx f1 + (sumIdx f3 + sumIdx f4) = dCoord Idx.r (fun r θ => sumIdx fun ρ => g M a ρ r θ * Γtot M r θ ρ Idx.θ b) r θ
branch_θ_merge :
  sumIdx f2 + (sumIdx f5 + sumIdx f6) = dCoord Idx.θ (fun r θ => sumIdx fun ρ => g M a ρ r θ * Γtot M r θ ρ Idx.r b) r θ
regroup_no2 :
  sumIdx f1 - sumIdx f2 + (sumIdx f3 + sumIdx f4) - (sumIdx f5 + sumIdx f6) =
    dCoord Idx.r (fun r θ => sumIdx fun ρ => g M a ρ r θ * Γtot M r θ ρ Idx.θ b) r θ -
      dCoord Idx.θ (fun r θ => sumIdx fun ρ => g M a ρ r θ * Γtot M r θ ρ Idx.r b) r θ
A : ℝ := sumIdx fun ρ => g M a ρ r θ * dCoord Idx.r (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ Idx.θ b) r θ
B : ℝ := sumIdx fun ρ => g M a ρ r θ * dCoord Idx.θ (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ Idx.r b) r θ
C : ℝ := sumIdx fun ρ => dCoord Idx.r (fun r θ => g M a ρ r θ) r θ * Γtot M r θ ρ Idx.θ b
D : ℝ := sumIdx fun ρ => dCoord Idx.θ (fun r θ => g M a ρ r θ) r θ * Γtot M r θ ρ Idx.r b
M_r : ℝ := sumIdx fun ρ => g M a ρ r θ * sumIdx fun lam => Γtot M r θ ρ Idx.r lam * Γtot M r θ lam Idx.θ b
M_θ : ℝ := sumIdx fun ρ => g M a ρ r θ * sumIdx fun lam => Γtot M r θ ρ Idx.θ lam * Γtot M r θ lam Idx.r b
Extra_r : ℝ := sumIdx fun lam => Γtot M r θ lam Idx.r a * Γ₁ M r θ lam Idx.θ b
Extra_θ : ℝ := sumIdx fun lam => Γtot M r θ lam Idx.θ a * Γ₁ M r θ lam Idx.r b
recog_Tθ : (sumIdx fun ρ => g M a ρ r θ * Γtot M r θ ρ Idx.θ b) = Γ₁ M r θ a Idx.θ b
recog_Tr : (sumIdx fun ρ => g M a ρ r θ * Γtot M r θ ρ Idx.r b) = Γ₁ M r θ a Idx.r b
hA_raw :
  (sumIdx fun ρ => g M a ρ r θ * dCoord Idx.r (fun r' θ' => Γtot M r' θ' ρ Idx.θ b) r θ) =
    dCoord Idx.r (fun r' θ' => sumIdx fun ρ => g M a ρ r' θ' * Γtot M r' θ' ρ Idx.θ b) r θ -
      sumIdx fun ρ => dCoord Idx.r (fun r' θ' => g M a ρ r' θ') r θ * Γtot M r θ ρ Idx.θ b
hA : A = dCoord Idx.r (fun r θ => Γ₁ M r θ a Idx.θ b) r θ - C
hB_raw :
  (sumIdx fun ρ => g M a ρ r θ * dCoord Idx.θ (fun r' θ' => Γtot M r' θ' ρ Idx.r b) r θ) =
    dCoord Idx.θ (fun r' θ' => sumIdx fun ρ => g M a ρ r' θ' * Γtot M r' θ' ρ Idx.r b) r θ -
      sumIdx fun ρ => dCoord Idx.θ (fun r' θ' => g M a ρ r' θ') r θ * Γtot M r θ ρ Idx.r b
hB : B = dCoord Idx.θ (fun r θ => Γ₁ M r θ a Idx.r b) r θ - D
dTθ_r : dCoord Idx.r (fun r θ => Γ₁ M r θ a Idx.θ b) r θ = A + C
dTr_θ : dCoord Idx.θ (fun r θ => Γ₁ M r θ a Idx.r b) r θ = B + D
recog_Tθ_fun : (fun r θ => sumIdx fun ρ => g M a ρ r θ * Γtot M r θ ρ Idx.θ b) = fun r θ => Γ₁ M r θ a Idx.θ b
recog_Tr_fun : (fun r θ => sumIdx fun ρ => g M a ρ r θ * Γtot M r θ ρ Idx.r b) = fun r θ => Γ₁ M r θ a Idx.r b
step0 :
  dCoord Idx.r (fun r θ => sumIdx fun ρ => g M a ρ r θ * Γtot M r θ ρ Idx.θ b) r θ -
      dCoord Idx.θ (fun r θ => sumIdx fun ρ => g M a ρ r θ * Γtot M r θ ρ Idx.r b) r θ =
    A - B + (C - D)
hC : C = M_r + Extra_r
hD : D = M_θ + Extra_θ
step1 : A - B + (C - D) = A - B + (M_r + Extra_r - (M_θ + Extra_θ))
step2 : A - B + (M_r + Extra_r - (M_θ + Extra_θ)) = A - B + (M_r - M_θ) + (Extra_r - Extra_θ)
f₁ : Idx → ℝ := fun ρ => g M a ρ r θ * dCoord Idx.r (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ Idx.θ b) r θ
f₂ : Idx → ℝ := fun ρ => g M a ρ r θ * dCoord Idx.θ (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ Idx.r b) r θ
f₃ : Idx → ℝ := fun ρ => g M a ρ r θ * sumIdx fun lam => Γtot M r θ ρ Idx.r lam * Γtot M r θ lam Idx.θ b
f₄ : Idx → ℝ := fun ρ => g M a ρ r θ * sumIdx fun lam => Γtot M r θ ρ Idx.θ lam * Γtot M r θ lam Idx.r b
step3 : A - B + (M_r - M_θ) = sumIdx fun ρ => f₁ ρ - f₂ ρ + f₃ ρ - f₄ ρ
ρ : Idx
⊢ True ∨
    (match (motive := Idx → Idx → ℝ → ℝ → ℝ) a, ρ with
        | t, t => fun r _θ => -f M r
        | Idx.r, Idx.r => fun r _θ => (f M r)⁻¹
        | Idx.θ, Idx.θ => fun r _θ => r ^ 2
        | φ, φ => fun r θ => r ^ 2 * sin θ ^ 2
        | x, x_1 => fun x x => 0)
        r θ =
      0

M r θ : ℝ
h_ext : Exterior M r θ
hθ : sin θ ≠ 0
μ ν a b : Idx
bb_core : ℝ :=
  sumIdx fun ρ =>
    g M ρ b r θ *
      ((sumIdx fun e => Γtot M r θ ρ ν e * Γtot M r θ e μ a) - sumIdx fun e => Γtot M r θ ρ μ e * Γtot M r θ e ν a)

  bb_core =
    sumIdx fun ρ =>
      g M ρ b r θ *
        ((sumIdx fun e => Γtot M r θ ρ ν e * Γtot M r θ e μ a) - sumIdx fun e => Γtot M r θ ρ μ e * Γtot M r θ e ν a)

  sumIdx fun ρ => g M ρ ρ r θ * (Γtot M r θ ρ μ a * Γtot M r θ ρ ν b - Γtot M r θ ρ ν a * Γtot M r θ ρ μ b)

  rho_core_a = sumIdx fun ρ => g M ρ ρ r θ * (Γtot M r θ ρ μ b * Γtot M r θ ρ ν a - Γtot M r θ ρ ν b * Γtot M r θ ρ μ a)
reshape :
  dCoord μ (fun r θ => nabla_g M r θ ν a b) r θ - Gamma_mu_nabla_nu M r θ μ ν a b -
      (dCoord ν (fun r θ => nabla_g M r θ μ a b) r θ - Gamma_nu_nabla_mu M r θ μ ν a b) =
    dCoord μ (fun r θ => nabla_g M r θ ν a b) r θ - dCoord ν (fun r θ => nabla_g M r θ μ a b) r θ -
        Gamma_mu_nabla_nu M r θ μ ν a b +
      Gamma_nu_nabla_mu M r θ μ ν a b
E :
  dCoord μ (fun r θ => nabla_g M r θ ν a b) r θ - dCoord ν (fun r θ => nabla_g M r θ μ a b) r θ =
    (sumIdx fun e =>
        -dCoord μ (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ e ν a) r θ * g M e b r θ +
              dCoord ν (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ e μ a) r θ * g M e b r θ -
            dCoord μ (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ e ν b) r θ * g M a e r θ +
          dCoord ν (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ e μ b) r θ * g M a e r θ) +
      sumIdx fun e =>
        -Γtot M r θ e ν a * dCoord μ (fun r θ => g M e b r θ) r θ +
              Γtot M r θ e μ a * dCoord ν (fun r θ => g M e b r θ) r θ -
            Γtot M r θ e ν b * dCoord μ (fun r θ => g M a e r θ) r θ +
          Γtot M r θ e μ b * dCoord ν (fun r θ => g M a e r θ) r θ
B_b : Idx → ℝ :=
  fun ρ =>
    -dCoord μ (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ ν a) r θ * g M ρ b r θ +
          dCoord ν (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ μ a) r θ * g M ρ b r θ -
        Γtot M r θ ρ ν a * dCoord μ (fun r θ => g M ρ b r θ) r θ +
      Γtot M r θ ρ μ a * dCoord ν (fun r θ => g M ρ b r θ) r θ
hBb :
  B_b = fun ρ =>
    -dCoord μ (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ ν a) r θ * g M ρ b r θ +
          dCoord ν (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ μ a) r θ * g M ρ b r θ -
        Γtot M r θ ρ ν a * dCoord μ (fun r θ => g M ρ b r θ) r θ +
      Γtot M r θ ρ μ a * dCoord ν (fun r θ => g M ρ b r θ) r θ
B_a : Idx → ℝ :=
  fun ρ =>
    -dCoord μ (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ ν b) r θ * g M a ρ r θ +

    -dCoord μ (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ ν a) r θ * g M ρ b r θ +

    -dCoord μ (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ ν a) r θ * g M ρ b r θ + dCoord ν (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ μ a) r θ * g M ρ b r θ

  fun ρ =>
    -dCoord μ (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ ν b) r θ * g M a ρ r θ + dCoord ν (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ μ b) r θ * g M a ρ r θ

  fun ρ =>
    -Γtot M r θ ρ ν a * dCoord μ (fun r θ => g M ρ b r θ) r θ + Γtot M r θ ρ μ a * dCoord ν (fun r θ => g M ρ b r θ) r θ

Cν_def : Gamma_nu_nabla_mu M r θ μ ν a b = Cνa + Cνb

    0

  -(((dCoord μ (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ b ν a) r θ - dCoord ν (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ b μ a) r θ +

    -dCoord μ (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ ν b) r θ * g M a ρ r θ +
          dCoord ν (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ μ b) r θ * g M a ρ r θ -

  fun ρ =>
    -dCoord μ (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ ν a) r θ * g M ρ b r θ + dCoord ν (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ μ a) r θ * g M ρ b r θ

  dG_b = fun ρ =>
    -dCoord μ (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ ν a) r θ * g M ρ b r θ + dCoord ν (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ μ a) r θ * g M ρ b r θ

  fun ρ =>

  dG_a = fun ρ =>
    -dCoord μ (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ ν b) r θ * g M a ρ r θ + dCoord ν (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ μ b) r θ * g M a ρ r θ
P_b : Idx → ℝ :=
  fun ρ =>
    -Γtot M r θ ρ ν a * dCoord μ (fun r θ => g M ρ b r θ) r θ + Γtot M r θ ρ μ a * dCoord ν (fun r θ => g M ρ b r θ) r θ

  P_b = fun ρ =>
    -Γtot M r θ ρ ν a * dCoord μ (fun r θ => g M ρ b r θ) r θ + Γtot M r θ ρ μ a * dCoord ν (fun r θ => g M ρ b r θ) r θ

  dCoord μ (fun r θ => nabla_g M r θ ν a b) r θ - dCoord ν (fun r θ => nabla_g M r θ μ a b) r θ =
    sumIdx B_b + sumIdx B_a

hCμa : Cμa = sumIdx fun ρ => Γtot M r θ ρ μ a * nabla_g M r θ ν ρ b

  (sumIdx fun ρ => Γtot M r θ ρ μ a * sumIdx fun e => Γtot M r θ e ν ρ * g M e b r θ) =
    sumIdx fun ρ => g M ρ b r θ * sumIdx fun e => Γtot M r θ ρ ν e * Γtot M r θ e μ a

Cν_def : Gamma_nu_nabla_mu M r θ μ ν a b = Cνa + Cνb

    0

h_rho_core_b :
  rho_core_b = sumIdx fun ρ => g M ρ ρ r θ * (Γtot M r θ ρ μ a * Γtot M r θ ρ ν b - Γtot M r θ ρ ν a * Γtot M r θ ρ μ b)
aa_core : ℝ :=
  sumIdx fun ρ =>
    g M ρ a r θ *
      ((sumIdx fun e => Γtot M r θ ρ ν e * Γtot M r θ e μ b) - sumIdx fun e => Γtot M r θ ρ μ e * Γtot M r θ e ν b)
h_aa_core :
  aa_core =
    sumIdx fun ρ =>
      g M ρ a r θ *
        ((sumIdx fun e => Γtot M r θ ρ ν e * Γtot M r θ e μ b) - sumIdx fun e => Γtot M r θ ρ μ e * Γtot M r θ e ν b)
rho_core_a : ℝ :=
  sumIdx fun ρ => g M ρ ρ r θ * (Γtot M r θ ρ μ b * Γtot M r θ ρ ν a - Γtot M r θ ρ ν b * Γtot M r θ ρ μ a)
h_rho_core_a :
  rho_core_a = sumIdx fun ρ => g M ρ ρ r θ * (Γtot M r θ ρ μ b * Γtot M r θ ρ ν a - Γtot M r θ ρ ν b * Γtot M r θ ρ μ a)
reshape :
  dCoord μ (fun r θ => nabla_g M r θ ν a b) r θ - Gamma_mu_nabla_nu M r θ μ ν a b -
      (dCoord ν (fun r θ => nabla_g M r θ μ a b) r θ - Gamma_nu_nabla_mu M r θ μ ν a b) =
    dCoord μ (fun r θ => nabla_g M r θ ν a b) r θ - dCoord ν (fun r θ => nabla_g M r θ μ a b) r θ -
        Gamma_mu_nabla_nu M r θ μ ν a b +
      Gamma_nu_nabla_mu M r θ μ ν a b
E :
  dCoord μ (fun r θ => nabla_g M r θ ν a b) r θ - dCoord ν (fun r θ => nabla_g M r θ μ a b) r θ =
    (sumIdx fun e =>
        -dCoord μ (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ e ν a) r θ * g M e b r θ +
              dCoord ν (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ e μ a) r θ * g M e b r θ -
            dCoord μ (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ e ν b) r θ * g M a e r θ +
          dCoord ν (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ e μ b) r θ * g M a e r θ) +
      sumIdx fun e =>
        -Γtot M r θ e ν a * dCoord μ (fun r θ => g M e b r θ) r θ +
              Γtot M r θ e μ a * dCoord ν (fun r θ => g M e b r θ) r θ -
            Γtot M r θ e ν b * dCoord μ (fun r θ => g M a e r θ) r θ +
          Γtot M r θ e μ b * dCoord ν (fun r θ => g M a e r θ) r θ
B_b : Idx → ℝ :=
  fun ρ =>
    -dCoord μ (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ ν a) r θ * g M ρ b r θ +
          dCoord ν (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ μ a) r θ * g M ρ b r θ -
        Γtot M r θ ρ ν a * dCoord μ (fun r θ => g M ρ b r θ) r θ +
      Γtot M r θ ρ μ a * dCoord ν (fun r θ => g M ρ b r θ) r θ
hBb :
  B_b = fun ρ =>
    -dCoord μ (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ ν a) r θ * g M ρ b r θ +
          dCoord ν (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ μ a) r θ * g M ρ b r θ -
        Γtot M r θ ρ ν a * dCoord μ (fun r θ => g M ρ b r θ) r θ +
      Γtot M r θ ρ μ a * dCoord ν (fun r θ => g M ρ b r θ) r θ
B_a : Idx → ℝ :=
  fun ρ =>
    -dCoord μ (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ ν b) r θ * g M a ρ r θ +
          dCoord ν (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ μ b) r θ * g M a ρ r θ -
        Γtot M r θ ρ ν b * dCoord μ (fun r θ => g M a ρ r θ) r θ +
      Γtot M r θ ρ μ b * dCoord ν (fun r θ => g M a ρ r θ) r θ
hBa :
  B_a = fun ρ =>
    -dCoord μ (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ ν b) r θ * g M a ρ r θ +
          dCoord ν (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ μ b) r θ * g M a ρ r θ -
        Γtot M r θ ρ ν b * dCoord μ (fun r θ => g M a ρ r θ) r θ +
      Γtot M r θ ρ μ b * dCoord ν (fun r θ => g M a ρ r θ) r θ
dG_b : Idx → ℝ :=
  fun ρ =>
    -dCoord μ (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ ν a) r θ * g M ρ b r θ + dCoord ν (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ μ a) r θ * g M ρ b r θ
hdGb :
  dG_b = fun ρ =>
    -dCoord μ (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ ν a) r θ * g M ρ b r θ + dCoord ν (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ μ a) r θ * g M ρ b r θ
dG_a : Idx → ℝ :=
  fun ρ =>
    -dCoord μ (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ ν b) r θ * g M a ρ r θ + dCoord ν (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ μ b) r θ * g M a ρ r θ
hdGa :
  dG_a = fun ρ =>
    -dCoord μ (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ ν b) r θ * g M a ρ r θ + dCoord ν (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ μ b) r θ * g M a ρ r θ
P_b : Idx → ℝ :=
  fun ρ =>
    -Γtot M r θ ρ ν a * dCoord μ (fun r θ => g M ρ b r θ) r θ + Γtot M r θ ρ μ a * dCoord ν (fun r θ => g M ρ b r θ) r θ
hPb :
  P_b = fun ρ =>
    -Γtot M r θ ρ ν a * dCoord μ (fun r θ => g M ρ b r θ) r θ + Γtot M r θ ρ μ a * dCoord ν (fun r θ => g M ρ b r θ) r θ
P_a : Idx → ℝ :=
  fun ρ =>
    -Γtot M r θ ρ ν b * dCoord μ (fun r θ => g M a ρ r θ) r θ + Γtot M r θ ρ μ b * dCoord ν (fun r θ => g M a ρ r θ) r θ
hPa :
  P_a = fun ρ =>
    -Γtot M r θ ρ ν b * dCoord μ (fun r θ => g M a ρ r θ) r θ + Γtot M r θ ρ μ b * dCoord ν (fun r θ => g M a ρ r θ) r θ
E' :
  dCoord μ (fun r θ => nabla_g M r θ ν a b) r θ - dCoord ν (fun r θ => nabla_g M r θ μ a b) r θ =
    sumIdx B_b + sumIdx B_a
Cμa : ℝ := sumIdx fun ρ => Γtot M r θ ρ μ a * nabla_g M r θ ν ρ b
hCμa : Cμa = sumIdx fun ρ => Γtot M r θ ρ μ a * nabla_g M r θ ν ρ b
Cμb : ℝ := sumIdx fun ρ => Γtot M r θ ρ μ b * nabla_g M r θ ν a ρ
hCμb : Cμb = sumIdx fun ρ => Γtot M r θ ρ μ b * nabla_g M r θ ν a ρ
Cνa : ℝ := sumIdx fun ρ => Γtot M r θ ρ ν a * nabla_g M r θ μ ρ b
hCνa : Cνa = sumIdx fun ρ => Γtot M r θ ρ ν a * nabla_g M r θ μ ρ b
Cνb : ℝ := sumIdx fun ρ => Γtot M r θ ρ ν b * nabla_g M r θ μ a ρ
hCνb : Cνb = sumIdx fun ρ => Γtot M r θ ρ ν b * nabla_g M r θ μ a ρ
ΓΓ_main_reindex_b_μ :
  (sumIdx fun ρ => Γtot M r θ ρ μ a * sumIdx fun e => Γtot M r θ e ν ρ * g M e b r θ) =
    sumIdx fun ρ => g M ρ b r θ * sumIdx fun e => Γtot M r θ ρ ν e * Γtot M r θ e μ a
ΓΓ_main_reindex_b_ν :
  (sumIdx fun ρ => Γtot M r θ ρ ν a * sumIdx fun e => Γtot M r θ e μ ρ * g M e b r θ) =
    sumIdx fun ρ => g M ρ b r θ * sumIdx fun e => Γtot M r θ ρ μ e * Γtot M r θ e ν a
ΓΓ_cross_collapse_b_μ :
  (sumIdx fun ρ => Γtot M r θ ρ μ a * sumIdx fun e => Γtot M r θ e ν b * g M ρ e r θ) =
    sumIdx fun ρ => g M ρ ρ r θ * (Γtot M r θ ρ μ a * Γtot M r θ ρ ν b)
ΓΓ_cross_collapse_b_ν :
  (sumIdx fun ρ => Γtot M r θ ρ ν a * sumIdx fun e => Γtot M r θ e μ b * g M ρ e r θ) =
    sumIdx fun ρ => g M ρ ρ r θ * (Γtot M r θ ρ ν a * Γtot M r θ ρ μ b)
ΓΓ_main_reindex_a_μ :
  (sumIdx fun ρ => Γtot M r θ ρ μ b * sumIdx fun e => Γtot M r θ e ν ρ * g M e a r θ) =
    sumIdx fun ρ => g M ρ a r θ * sumIdx fun e => Γtot M r θ ρ ν e * Γtot M r θ e μ b
ΓΓ_main_reindex_a_ν :
  (sumIdx fun ρ => Γtot M r θ ρ ν b * sumIdx fun e => Γtot M r θ e μ ρ * g M e a r θ) =
    sumIdx fun ρ => g M ρ a r θ * sumIdx fun e => Γtot M r θ ρ μ e * Γtot M r θ e ν b
ΓΓ_cross_collapse_a_μ :
  (sumIdx fun ρ => Γtot M r θ ρ μ b * sumIdx fun e => Γtot M r θ e ν a * g M ρ e r θ) =
    sumIdx fun ρ => g M ρ ρ r θ * (Γtot M r θ ρ μ b * Γtot M r θ ρ ν a)
ΓΓ_cross_collapse_a_ν :
  (sumIdx fun ρ => Γtot M r θ ρ ν b * sumIdx fun e => Γtot M r θ e μ a * g M ρ e r θ) =
    sumIdx fun ρ => g M ρ ρ r θ * (Γtot M r θ ρ ν b * Γtot M r θ ρ μ a)
Cμ_def : Gamma_mu_nabla_nu M r θ μ ν a b = Cμa + Cμb
Cν_def : Gamma_nu_nabla_mu M r θ μ ν a b = Cνa + Cνb
LHS_small :
  dCoord μ (fun r θ => nabla_g M r θ ν a b) r θ - Gamma_mu_nabla_nu M r θ μ ν a b -
      (dCoord ν (fun r θ => nabla_g M r θ μ a b) r θ - Gamma_nu_nabla_mu M r θ μ ν a b) =
    sumIdx B_b + sumIdx B_a - (Cμa + Cμb) + (Cνa + Cνb)
regroup : sumIdx B_b + sumIdx B_a - (Cμa + Cμb) + (Cνa + Cνb) = sumIdx B_b - Cμa + Cνa + (sumIdx B_a - Cμb + Cνb)
hb_pack :
  sumIdx B_b - Cμa + Cνa =
    sumIdx fun ρ => B_b ρ - Γtot M r θ ρ μ a * nabla_g M r θ ν ρ b + Γtot M r θ ρ ν a * nabla_g M r θ μ ρ b
hb :
  ((sumIdx B_b - sumIdx fun ρ => Γtot M r θ ρ μ a * nabla_g M r θ ν ρ b) +
      sumIdx fun ρ => Γtot M r θ ρ ν a * nabla_g M r θ μ ρ b) =
    -sumIdx fun ρ => RiemannUp M r θ ρ a μ ν * g M ρ b r θ
ha_pack :
  sumIdx B_a - Cμb + Cνb =
    sumIdx fun ρ => B_a ρ - Γtot M r θ ρ μ b * nabla_g M r θ ν a ρ + Γtot M r θ ρ ν b * nabla_g M r θ μ a ρ
payload_cancel :
  (sumIdx fun ρ =>
      -Γtot M r θ ρ ν b * dCoord μ (fun r θ => g M a ρ r θ) r θ +
          Γtot M r θ ρ μ b * dCoord ν (fun r θ => g M a ρ r θ) r θ -
        (Γtot M r θ ρ μ b * dCoord ν (fun r θ => g M a ρ r θ) r θ -
          Γtot M r θ ρ ν b * dCoord μ (fun r θ => g M a ρ r θ) r θ)) =
    0
ΓΓ_block :
  ((sumIdx fun ρ => Γtot M r θ ρ μ b * sumIdx fun e => Γtot M r θ e ν ρ * g M e a r θ) -
        sumIdx fun ρ => Γtot M r θ ρ ν b * sumIdx fun e => Γtot M r θ e μ ρ * g M e a r θ) +
      ((sumIdx fun ρ => Γtot M r θ ρ μ b * sumIdx fun e => Γtot M r θ e ν a * g M ρ e r θ) -
        sumIdx fun ρ => Γtot M r θ ρ ν b * sumIdx fun e => Γtot M r θ e μ a * g M ρ e r θ) =
    aa_core + rho_core_a
scalar_finish_aa :
  -dCoord μ (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ a ν b) r θ * g M a a r θ + dCoord ν (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ a μ b) r θ * g M a a r θ +
      g M a a r θ *
        ((sumIdx fun e => Γtot M r θ a μ e * Γtot M r θ e ν b) - sumIdx fun e => Γtot M r θ a ν e * Γtot M r θ e μ b) =
    (-dCoord μ (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ a ν b) r θ + dCoord ν (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ a μ b) r θ +
        ((sumIdx fun e => Γtot M r θ a μ e * Γtot M r θ e ν b) - sumIdx fun e => Γtot M r θ a ν e * Γtot M r θ e μ b)) *
      g M a a r θ
core_as_sum_a :
  -(((dCoord μ (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ a ν b) r θ - dCoord ν (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ a μ b) r θ +
            sumIdx fun e => Γtot M r θ a μ e * Γtot M r θ e ν b) -
          sumIdx fun e => Γtot M r θ a ν e * Γtot M r θ e μ b) *
        g M a a r θ) =
    sumIdx fun ρ =>
      -(((dCoord μ (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ ν b) r θ - dCoord ν (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ μ b) r θ +
                sumIdx fun e => Γtot M r θ ρ μ e * Γtot M r θ e ν b) -
              sumIdx fun e => Γtot M r θ ρ ν e * Γtot M r θ e μ b) *
            g M a ρ r θ) *
        if ρ = a then 1 else 0
scalar_finish :
  ∀ (ρ : Idx),
    -dCoord μ (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ ν b) r θ * g M a ρ r θ +
          dCoord ν (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ μ b) r θ * g M a ρ r θ +
        g M a ρ r θ *
          ((sumIdx fun e => Γtot M r θ ρ μ e * Γtot M r θ e ν b) -
            sumIdx fun e => Γtot M r θ ρ ν e * Γtot M r θ e μ b) =
      -(((dCoord μ (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ ν b) r θ - dCoord ν (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ μ b) r θ +
              sumIdx fun e => Γtot M r θ ρ μ e * Γtot M r θ e ν b) -
            sumIdx fun e => Γtot M r θ ρ ν e * Γtot M r θ e μ b) *
          g M a ρ r θ)
⊢ (-sumIdx fun ρ => RiemannUp M r θ ρ b μ ν * g M a ρ r θ) + rho_core_a =
    -sumIdx fun ρ =>
        (dCoord μ (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ ν b) r θ + -dCoord ν (fun r θ => Γtot M r θ ρ μ b) r θ +
            sumIdx fun lam => Γtot M r θ ρ μ lam * Γtot M r θ lam ν b + -(Γtot M r θ ρ ν lam * Γtot M r θ lam μ b)) *
          g M a ρ r θ
